I've been coming here for my pho fix since they opened never have I had such bad service up until this past week. I walked in to place an order to go and payed for my order. They told me it be about 40 min so I went home and returned. I gave them extra time and began my 40 min wait once I got home and left a few min later to ensure my irse would be ready. When I arrived the guy seen me and frantically begins to look for my order slip . Then another guy comes from the back to ask what my order was. I kindly repeat my order. Sadly enough my order was clearly forgotten and hadn't been made. I was told my order would be right up. I waited an additional 30 min sitting there waiting on my order. Honestly I wish I would've paid cash because with that wait I would've asked for my money back and would've taken my business elsewhere. Will I return ... never and I always would recommend this restaurant to anyone asking for a good place to eat. Listen, as a young woman this was the best service I‚Äôve ever had! Long winded but keep reading...

I got into a car accident a few months back in Atlanta and had Abra Body (Caliber Collision in GA) fix my car. I was relocating to CA soon and wanted to make sure everything was okay with my vehicle driving it so many miles across country.

I‚Äôm the middle of the 31 hour drive, my gas light came on and eventually my check engine. I tried not to panic, especially when I realized Abra (Caliber Collision) was in California too, but at the same time I was frustrated not knowing even with the the lifetime warranty whether or not they would take care of/take responsibility/ or even fix my car!

The first place I looked up was in Pasadena and when I walked in, Viviana (Front Desk Rep), was soooo nice to me! Eddie took a look at my car and after about 20 mins got me into a rental so I can continue with my day and they could fix the problem! This helped me especially being a young women in a new city with a car needing to be fixed! After a week and a half, I‚Äôm picking up my car and I‚Äôm a happy girl! My car drives perfect!

<review>I've been on the search for a new Dentist and tend to steer away from dental chain groups or large offices based on my preference and experiences with dental offices. I did some searching on local providers and was pleased with the positive feedback prior patients and colleagues had to say.

Dr. Catherine Irasusta has now been my new Dentist for just under a month and couldn't be more happy with my choice for a new Dentist. I've included some of the key things I personally pay attention to when visiting a office. I've been to the office about 4 times as of this review .

- Office Cleanliness: The office waiting area/lobby has been very clean the few times I've been in so far as well as nicely decorated and inviting. And as of recent, nicely decorated with Christmas decorations and like who doesn‚Äôt like Christmas Decorations during the happiest time of the year!? Magazines are also available to browse through while you wait which by the way (won‚Äôt be long)..

- Wait Time: This is always a make or break for an office. I'm pleased to say my last four visits have always been right on time as scheduled, my most recent appointment was even called back 5 minutes prior to the scheduled time which is a plus!

- Office Staff: Dr.Irasusta has an amazing team! Starting with the front desk staff which are always friendly and great at explaining any questions you may have pertaining to your insurance/ and any out-of-pocket costs you may have. The dental assistants and hygienist are really great too! Overall have had great experiences with the staff.

- Quality of Care: Most importantly, Quality of Care? Dr. Irasusta is extremely thorough in examining your teeth. She provides a clear treatment plan, answers and explains and questions/concerns you may have and she's also very friendly and personable! You will definitely take notice of how experienced and knowledgeable she is.

Overall I'm extremely satisfied with my choice in leaving my Dental Care with Dr. Irasusta and her staff. If you're searching for a new Dentist or perhaps don't feel like you're getting the service in some of the key points I've noted. I'd definitely recommend to give their office a call and schedule an appointment!

Thank you Doctor Irasusta and staff for making me feel GREAT when I smile! You all are amazing!!

<Rating>1<//Rating>< Review>
Wanted to share my experience.  I ordered a to-go item with butter nan.  I picked up the item and by the time I reached home (around 10 mins), I noticed that Nan had become very hard and was not edible.  I could not eat it.  I called this restaurant to inform about the the Nan.  I was expecting an apology.  Instead of that the manager (I think name was Samar or something) started kind of lecturing me that Nans are made that way as If I have never eaten one.  The tone of manager was as if customer was lying about problem with Nan.  I understand that there are subjective things such as taste of food  etc where you could argue with customer (even then it is a bad idea),  but Nan being too hard is demonstrable fact and there was no need to argue.

A very basic rule in restaurant business is (or any business) to hear customer's criticism and improve.  Also if customer is calling about the quality of food or service,  make amends and not argue.  Any restaurant business that blames customers for quality of food does not know the basic rules of running restaurant business.

I think owner of this business has hired incompetent manager and other staff to run his business.  Unhappy customers would go to other places specially in Bay area where there is no shortage of Indian restaurants.</Review>

5</rate>
< Review>
This rating is based solely off of one dish that they prepare: Vijayawada Chicken Biryani, aka the best Biryani in the Bay area and arguably my entire Biryani experience.

If you're from the area, you know how many options there are for good Indian food, so you'll understand when I say that I only go to each place for a couple exemplary dishes (not the whole menu). Well for Tabla, that's the Biryani mentioned above!

Don't come for the dining experience, the ambiance, the service or the music. Come for the only thing that matters here, the Biryani!

The aroma is enticing, smelling strongly of a refined selection of rich Indian spices. Unlike many styles, this one has the rice on top and the chicken baked underneath (of which there is a surprisingly good amount). Large portions, soaked in a fantastic curry accompaniment, you just can't go wrong with this one. The spice level is great - not too much so as to make those with low tolerances cry but enough to make the more acclimated stop intermittently and appreciate the flavor (while giving their tongue a quick rest). Plus the raita is perfect to help relieve the burn (and alleviate digestion troubles by protectively lining the stomach).

As mentioned, I can't speak towards the dining experience, or really the rest of the menu (except for some unsurprisingly mediocre tandoori chicken).

My sole recommendation is that you order the Vijayawada Chicken Biryani! And if you're like me, get an extra to go (because it only gets better).< /Review>

<review>UPDATED REVIEW
----------------------------
Reducing to 3 stars. I have been here 5-6 times during lunch and every time I have experienced it.
The pressure cooker whistle starts off all of a sudden and its pretty loud. It goes on for a minute at a stretch at least. And it goes off 4 -5 times one after the other. I think you can imagine how the experience gets like when you are eating and at times it gets too annoying. You can't even hear what's the guy next to you is saying.
To the owner, I am sure you can come up with a better plan to get rid of the whistles when people are having their lunch. Just soften the lentils (or whatever it is) beforehead !!!

ORIGINAL REVIEW
----------------------------
Quite a bit of food in the price.
They have complimentary Indian milk tea as well which tastes great.
I had ordered for the Non veg thali which came with 3 non veg curries (2 chicken and a goat curry), a daal, a rasam, yoghurt, yellow rice, plenty of white rice, naan, sweet, papad.
I was not able to complete the thali and the food tasted great.
I was happy to see that they serve fresh chapati as well. The seats and tables needs to be lot more cleaner.
